class op5_loop_body:
    var_ranges = {p0: 500, p1: 128, p2: 128}
    index0 = 16384*p0 + 128*p1 + p2
    index1 = 128*p0 + p1
    index2 = p2
    index3 = 128*p0 + 64000*p1 + p2
    def body(self, ops):
        get_index = self.get_index('index0')
        load = ops.load('buf0', get_index)
        get_index_1 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_1 = ops.load('buf1', get_index_1)
        sub = ops.sub(load, load_1)
        get_index_2 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_2 = ops.load('buf4', get_index_2)
        mul = ops.mul(sub, load_2)
        get_index_3 = self.get_index('index2')
        load_3 = ops.load('primals_4', get_index_3)
        mul_1 = ops.mul(mul, load_3)
        get_index_4 = self.get_index('index2')
        load_4 = ops.load('primals_5', get_index_4)
        add = ops.add(mul_1, load_4)
        get_index_5 = self.get_index('index3')
        store = ops.store('buf5', get_index_5, add, None)
        return store

class op32_loop_body:
    var_ranges = {p0: 500, p1: 128, p2: 128}
    index0 = 16384*p0 + 128*p1 + p2
    index1 = 128*p0 + p1
    def body(self, ops):

        load = ops.load('buf28', get_index)
        get_index_1 = self.get_index('index1')
        load_1 = ops.load('buf29', get_index_1)
        sub = ops.sub(load, load_1)
        get_index_2 = self.get_index('index1')

        truediv = ops.truediv(load_2, constant)
        constant_1 = ops.constant(1e-05, torch.float32)

        rsqrt = ops.rsqrt(add)
        mul = ops.mul(sub, rsqrt)

        store = ops.store('buf32', get_index_3, mul, None)
        return store
